font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">1 <o:p></o:p></span></div></td>  </tr>\r\n</tbody></table><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Those substances which have a viscosity equal to or greater than <span style=\"color: red; font-size: small;\">50 mPa.s at 20\u00b0C</span> shall be washed with hot water (temperature at least 60\u00b0C), unless the properties of such substances make the washing less effective. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM43\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Prewash procedures for non-Solidifying Substances </span></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">: Tanks shall be washed by means of a rotary water jet, operated at sufficiently high water pressure. In the case of <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">Category X</b> substances cleaning machines shall be operated in such locations that all tank surfaces are washed. In the case of <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">Category Y</b> substances only one location need be used. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM43\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Recycled medium prewash\u2014Can be adopted for washing more than one tank. The cargo concentration in the water / medium 5% based on stripping test quantities of the P&amp;A manual.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Every <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">ship constructed on or after 1 July 1986 but before 1 January 2007</b> shall be provided with a pumping and piping arrangement to ensure that each tank certified for the carriage of substances in <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">Category X or Y does not retain a quantity of residue in excess of 100 litres</b> in the tank and its associated piping<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM20\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">The definition of high viscosity in the revised Annex II would mean that a lot of vegetable oils (primarily the soft oils) could be required to be prewashed. <o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"CM20\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">It has been suggested that for certain oils, such as Soyabean oil, the discharge temperature could be raised slightly to bring the product out of the high viscosity range, thus obviating the need for a prewash, and the vegetable oil industry has been considering the issue. FEDIOL (the European refiners association) have, however, recently advised that they are not prepared to alter the heating instructions in respect of vegetable oils. This will mean that a prewash is inevitable for a number of oils. <o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"CM20\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">It should be noted that the revised Annex II requires that the prewash and discharge ashore should be carried out in the port of unloading unless a port that the vessel is due to call at later has confirmed in writing that it has a reception facility available that is adequate for the purpose. The unloaded tank must be neither washed nor ballasted at sea before the prewash can be carried out. <o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"CM19\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Prudent masters must ensure <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>the availability of shore reception facilities, till all are familiar will the new regulations. <o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Regarding the DH ( discharge temperature ), --for solidifying or high viscosity cargoes which have been identified as being required to be a certain minimum temperature during unloading--<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>If<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>P-Xylene was discharged at temperature of 17</span><span style=\"font-family: Symbol; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\"><span style=\"mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\">\u00b0</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">C,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>the tank cleaning slop of the cargo should be discharged to a reception facility because it is a solidifying cargo defined as Solidifying substance.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">It means --in case of substances with melting points less than 15</span><span style=\"font-family: Symbol; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\"><span style=\"mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\">\u00b0</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">C, is at a temperature, at the time of unloading, of less than 5</span><span style=\"font-family: Symbol; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\"><span style=\"mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\">\u00b0</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">C above its melting point.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Therefore the P-Xylene(melting point:13</span><span style=\"font-family: Symbol; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\"><span style=\"mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\">\u00b0</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">C) with temperature of<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>more than18</span><span style=\"font-family: Symbol; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\"><span style=\"mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\">\u00b0</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">C(13+5)<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>has<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>to be unloaded and then the tank cleaning slop of the cargo can be discharged into sea.<o:p></o:p></span></div><h1 style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: normal; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Category Z</span></b></span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\"> \u2013</span></b></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"> <o:p></o:p></span></h1><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"> </span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Noxious Liquid Substances which, if discharged into the sea from tank cleaning or deballasting operations, are deemed to present a minor hazard to either marine resources or human health and therefore justify less stringent restrictions on the quality and quantity of the discharge into the marine environment; <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Examples are <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Acetone, Acetic acid, Dodecyl Benzene , Methyl Ethyl Ketone, MTBE, Phosphoric acid , Urea <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>etc. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">For ships constructed before 1 January 2007</span></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"> the discharge into the sea of residues of substances in Category Z or of those provisionally assessed as such or ballast water, tank washings or other mixtures containing such substances <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">below the waterline is not mandatory. <o:p></o:p></b></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><br />\n</b></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">If the unloading of a substance of Category Y or Z is not carried out in accordance with the Manual, <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">a prewash shall be carried out</b> before the ship leaves the port of unloading. Remember this relates to unpumpables due to heating breakdown ( cold interface etc ) and excess ROB due to use of PORTABLE FRAMO etc. The resulting tank washings of the prewash shall be discharged to a reception facility at the port of unloading <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">or another port</b> with a suitable reception facility provided that it has been confirmed in writing that a reception facility at that port is available and is adequate for such a purpose. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Every <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">ship constructed on or after 1 July 1986 but before 1 January 2007</b> shall be provided with a pumping and piping arrangement to ensure that each tank certified for the carriage of substances in <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">Category Z</b> does not retain a quantity of residue in excess of <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">300 litres</b> in the tank and its associated piping. If the stripping has failed or portable framo has been used for discharge due to deepwell pump failure , then the subject tanks have to be prewashed ( extended one ).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">For a ship other than a chemical tanker constructed before 1 January 2007 which cannot meet the requirements for the pumping and piping arrangements for substances in Category Z referred to in paragraphs 1 and 2 of this regulation no quantity requirement shall apply. Compliance is deemed to be reached if the tank is emptied to the most practicable extent.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Ships certified to carry substances of Category X, Y or Z shall have an underwater discharge outlet (or outlets). <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">For ships constructed before 1 January 2007 and certified to carry substances in Category Z an underwater discharge outlet is not mandatory. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;O &nbsp; &nbsp;Other</span>&nbsp;Substances</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">: <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>Substances indicated as OS (Other Substances) in the pollution category column of chapter 18 of the International Bulk Chemical Code which have been evaluated and found to fall outside Category X, Y or Z because they are, at present, considered to present no harm to marine resources, human health, amenities or other legitimate uses of the sea when discharged into the sea from tank cleaning of deballasting operations. The discharge of bilge or ballast water or other residues or mixtures containing only substances referred to as \u201cOther Substances\u201d shall not be subject to any requirements of the Annex. The fourth category, OS (Other Substances), contains only 8 harmless products (apple juice, clay slurry, coal slurry, dextrose solution, glucose solution, kaoline slurry, molasses, water).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">The revised annex includes a number of other significant changes. Improvements in ship technology, such as efficient stripping techniques, has made possible significantly lower permitted discharge levels of certain products which have been incorporated into Annex II. <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">For ships constructed on or after 1 January 2007 </b>the maximum permitted residue in the tank and its associated piping left after discharge will be set at a maximum of<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"> 75 litres</b> for products in categories<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"> X, Y and Z</b> - compared with previous limits which set a maximum of 100 or 300 litres (with 50 litres tolerance ), depending on the product category. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">After 1<sup>st</sup> January 2007, all vegetable oils which is being currently listed in Chapter 18 of the IBC code ( meaning that they can be carried in normal product tankers with NLS certificate) can only be carried on type 2 chemical tankers. This means these cargoes will be transferred from Chapter 18 to Chapter 17. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Depth of water means the charted depth.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM3\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">En route means that the ship is under way at sea on a course or courses, including deviation from the shortest direct route, which as far as practicable for navigational purposes, will cause any discharge to be spread over as great an area of the sea as is reasonable and practicable. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Liquid substances are those having a vapour pressure not exceeding 0.28 MPa absolute at a temperature of 37.8\u00b0C. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Nearest land. The term \u201cfrom the nearest land\u201d means from the baseline from which the territorial sea in question is established in accordance with international law<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Noxious Liquid Substance means any substance indicated in the Pollution Category column of chapter 17 or 18 of the International Bulk Chemical Code or provisionally assessed under the provisions of regulation 6.3 as falling into Category X, Y or Z.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">PPM means ml/m<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">3</span></sup>. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Residue means any noxious liquid substance which remains for disposal. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM6\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Residue/water mixture means residue to which water has been added for any purpose <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">The discharge requirements of this Annex shall not apply to the discharge into the sea of Noxious Liquid Substances or mixtures containing such substances when such a discharge: <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>is necessary for the purpose of safety of a ship or saving life at sea; or <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">results from damage to a ship or its equipment: <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">provided that all reasonable precautions have been taken after the occurrence of the damage or discovery of the discharge for the purpose of preventing or minimizing the discharge; and <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">except if the owner or the master acted either with intent to cause damage, or recklessly and with knowledge that damage would probably result; or<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">is approved by the Administration, when being used for the purpose of combating specific pollution incidents in order to minimize the damage from pollution. Any such discharge shall be subject to the approval of any Government in whose jurisdiction it is contemplated the discharge will occur.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Where the provisions in this regulation allow the discharge into the sea of residues of substances in <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">Category X, Y or Z</b> or of those provisionally assessed as such or ballast water, tank washings or other mixtures containing such substances the following discharge standards shall apply: </span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">1 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the ship is proceeding en route at a speed of at least 7 knots in the case of self-propelled ships or at least 4 knots in the case of ships which are not self-propelled; <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">2 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the discharge is made <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">below the waterline</i></b> through the underwater discharge outlet(s) not exceeding the maximum rate for which the underwater discharge outlet(s) is (are) designed; ( use of UW discharge is not mandatory for category Z residues and tankwashings )<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">3 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the discharge is made at a distance of not less than 12 nautical miles from the nearest land in a depth of water of not less than 25 metres. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">4<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Remark: the thing to note is that the discharge PPM is unrestricted after 1.1.07<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">For ships c<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">onstructed before 1 January 2007 </b>the discharge into the sea of residues of substances in <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">Category Z</b> or of those provisionally assessed as such or ballast water, tank washings or other mixtures containing such substances <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">below the waterline is not mandatory.</b> </span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">For Category Z, regarding the distance of not less than 12 nautical miles from the nearest land for ships solely engaged in voyages within waters subject to the sovereignty or jurisdiction of the State the flag, of which, the ship is entitled to fly. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">On request of the ship\u2019s master an exemption for a prewash may be granted by the Government of the receiving Party, where it is satisfied that: <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">1 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the unloaded tank is to be reloaded with the same substance or another substance compatible with the previous one and that the tank will not be washed or ballasted prior to loading; or <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">2<span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the unloaded tank is neither washed nor ballasted at sea. The prewash in accordance with the applicable paragraph of this regulation shall be carried out at another port provided that it has been confirmed in writing that a reception facility at that port is available and is adequate for such a purpose; or <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">3 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the cargo residues will be removed by a ventilation procedure approved by the Administration <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">When a washing medium other than water, such as mineral oil or chlorinated solvent, is used instead of water to wash a tank, its discharge shall be governed by the provisions of either Annex I or Annex II, which would apply to the medium had it been carried as cargo.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Tank washing procedures involving the use of such a medium shall be set out in the Manual and be approved by the Administration. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM3\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">When small amounts of cleaning additives (detergent products) are added to water in order to facilitate tank washing, no additives containing Pollution Category X components shall be used except those components that are readily biodegradable and present in a total concentration of less than 10% of the cleaning additive. No restrictions additional to those applicable to the tank due to the previous cargo shall apply. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Ballast introduced into a cargo tank which has been washed to such an extent that the ballast contains less than 1 ppm of the substance previously carried, may be discharged into the sea without regard to the discharge rate, ship\u2019s speed and discharge outlet location, provided that the ship is not less than 12 miles from the nearest land and in water that is not less than 25 metres deep.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Cargo record book <o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">After completion of any operation it shall be promptly recorded in the Cargo Record Book. In the event of an accidental discharge of a noxious liquid substance<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>an entry in ENGLISH <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>shall be made in the Cargo Record Book stating the circumstances of, and the reason for, the discharge. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Each entry shall be signed by the officer or officers in charge of the operation concerned and each page shall be signed by the master of the ship. The Cargo Record Book shall be kept in such a place as to be readily available for inspection .. It shall be retained for a period of three years after the last entry has been made.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The competent authority of the Government may inspect the Cargo Record Book on board any ship to which this Annex applies while the ship is in its port, and may make a copy of any entry in that book and may require the master of the ship to certify that the copy is a true copy of such entry. Any copy so made which has been certified by the master of the ship as a true copy of an entry in the ship\u2019s Cargo Record Book shall be made admissible in any judicial proceedings as evidence of the facts stated in the entry.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The inspection of a Cargo Record Book and the taking of a certified copy by the competent authority under this paragraph shall be performed as expeditiously as possible without causing the ship to be unduly delayed. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">The Government of each Party to the Convention shall appoint or authorize surveyors for the purpose of implementing this regulation. When a surveyor appointed or authorized by the Government of the Party to the Convention has verified that an operation has been carried out in accordance with the requirements of the Manual, or has granted an exemption for a prewash, then that surveyor shall make an appropriate entry in the Cargo Record Book. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Where it is impracticable to measure the concentration of the substance in the effluent without causing undue delay to the ship,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>the alternative procedure is for the surveyor to certify in the Cargo Record Book that: <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">1 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the tank, its pump and piping systems have been emptied; and <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">2 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the prewash has been carried out in accordance with the provisions of appendix 6 of this Annex; and <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">3 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the tank washing resulting from such prewash have been discharged to a reception facility and the tank is empty. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Minimum quantity of water to be used in a prewash <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">The minimum quantity of water to be used in a prewash is determined by the residual quantity of noxious liquid substance in the tank, the tank size, the cargo properties, the permitted concentration in any subsequent wash water effluent, and the area of operation. The minimum quantity is given by the following formula: <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Q=k(15r<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">0.8</span></sup><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>+ 5r<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">0.7</span></sup><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>x V/1000) <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>where Q = the required minimum quantity in m<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">3 </span></sup><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify; text-indent: -1in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>r = <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the residual quantity per tank in m<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">3</span></sup>. The value of r shall be the value demonstrated in the actual stripping efficiency test, but shall not be taken lower than 0.100 m<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">3</span></sup><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>for a tank volume of 500 m<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">3</span></sup><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>and above and 0.040 m<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">3 </span></sup>for a tank volume of 100 m<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">3</span></sup><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>and below. For tank sizes between 100 m<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">3</span></sup><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>and 500 m<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">3</span></sup><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>the minimum value of r allowed to be used in the calculations is obtained by linear interpolation. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">For Category X substances the value of r shall either be determined based on stripping tests according to the Manual, observing the lower limits as given above, or be taken to be 0.9 m<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">3</span></sup>. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify; text-indent: -1in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>V = <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>tank volume in m<sup><span style=\"mso-text-raise: 5.5pt; position: relative; top: -5.5pt;\">3 </span></sup><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">k = <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>a factor having values as follows: <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Category X, non-Solidifying, Low-Viscosity Substance, k = 1.2 <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Category X, Solidifying or High-Viscosity Substance, k = 2.4 <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Category Y, non-Solidifying, Low-Viscosity Substance<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>k = 0.5 <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM40\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Category Y, Solidifying or High-Viscosity Substance, k = 1.0 <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM47\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM47\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">The table below is calculated using the formula with a k factor of 1 and may be used as an easy reference. </span><br />\n</div><table border=\"1\" cellpadding=\"0\" cellspacing=\"0\" class=\"MsoNormalTable\" style=\"border-collapse: collapse; </span>The prewash volume so verified shall be adjusted for other prewash conditions by application of the factor k as defined in paragraph.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Ventilation of cargo residues from a tank : <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">High Volatile Cargoes with a VP&gt;5000 Pa @ 20 deg c ( 50 mb @ 20 deg c ) that can be removed by ventilation.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>1 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the pipelines shall be drained and further cleared of liquid by means of ventilation equipment; <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">2 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the list and trim shall be adjusted to the minimum levels possible so that evaporation of residues in the tank is enhanced; <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">3 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>ventilation equipment producing an airjet which can reach the tank bottom shall be used. Figure 7-1 could be used to evaluate the adequacy of ventilation equipment used for ventilating a tank of a given depth; <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">4 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>ventilation equipment shall be placed in the tank opening closest to the tank sump or suction point; <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM41\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">5 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>ventilation equipment shall, when practicable, be positioned so that the airjet is directed at the tank sump or suction point and impingement of the airjet on tank structural members is to be avoided as much as possible; and <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM8\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">6 <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>ventilation shall continue until no visible remains of liquid can be observed in the tank. This shall be verified by a visual examination or an equivalent method. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">The graph with inlet jet penetration depth in metres on X axis and minimum flow for each cargo tank in CUM/ min on Y axid is given in P&amp;A manual\u2014read off flow rate against linear lines for various inlet diameters </span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">CARGO RECORD BOOK:--<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoBodyText\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Every chemical tanker is required to maintain a Cargo Record Book. This book must be upto date at all times. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoBodyText\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoBodyText\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">In some ports (like in Algeria) the harbour master takes the cargo record book away while the ship is alongside and returns it just prior sailing . This is not allowed as per the regulations. Many ships are not familiar with<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>how to make correct entries in the Cargo Record Book .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Entries in the Cargo Record Book are required <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">only for operations involving Categories X,Y,Z substances</b><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><u>.</u><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></i>Other Substances carried in bulk are not subject to the provisions of this Annex as they are not in the Pollution Category column of chapters 17 of IBC Code and it is <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">NOT necessary to enter in the Cargo Record Book</b> (i.e.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Molasses, Clay slurry , Apple juice etc)</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left: 0in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .25in; text-align: left; text-indent: -0.25in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">The Cargo Record Book shall be completed, on a tank-to-tank basis, whenever any of the following operations<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Each operation shall be fully recorded <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">without delay</b> in the Cargo Record Book so that all the entries in the book appropriate to that operation are completed as and when it happened.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left: 0in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .25in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.25in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-list: Ignore;\">3.<span style=\"font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font: 7pt/normal &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">When making entries in the Cargo Record Book, the date, operational code and item number shall be inserted in the appropriate columns and the required particulars shall be recorded chronologically in the blank spaces <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">without leaving blank spaces</b> between last operation records and next operation records.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left: 0in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .25in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.25in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Each completed entry shall be signed by the officer in charge ( xxx ships Chief Officer ) and each completed page shall be countersigned by the master of the ship as soon as it is complete.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left: 0in; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Entries shall not be altered, erased, or cut in any case.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>If correction has to be made, two lines shall be run through such entry, leaving the corrected part in legible state, with the signature of the officer affixed. No tipex white fluid corrector can be used.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left: 0in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in; mso-line-height-alt: 10.35pt;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Any fuel made from a renewable biological source is considered a biofuel---</span></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">&nbsp;unlike other natural resources such as petroleum, coal and nuclear fuels.</span><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in; mso-line-height-alt: 10.35pt;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">The term \"biofuel\" encompasses a diverse range of products such as biogas, biodiesel (methyl ester of vegetable oils) and bio-ethanol, and also includes ethanol, and methanol.&nbsp;&nbsp;Liquid biofuels are mainly developed as a vehicle fuel.<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in; mso-line-height-alt: 10.35pt;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><br />\n</b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 10.0pt; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Chemical tanker officers must be familiar with BIODIESEL , as carriage of this cargo on chemical tankers will soon be commonplace. Biodiesel is a generic name for fuels obtained by trans \u2013esterification of a veg oil or animal fat.<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in; mso-line-height-alt: 10.35pt;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">There is no need for your COF to list the individual vegetable grades like Rapeseed FAME, Soya Bean FAME , Palm oil FAME etc.<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in; mso-line-height-alt: 10.35pt;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><br />\n</b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Fatty Acid Methyl Esters have now been accepted as a generic term for the carriage of Biodiesel under the revised&nbsp;&nbsp;MARPOL Annex II, provided they are derived from vegetable oils already found in the IBC Code under Ch 17, Marpol Pollution Category Y and Ship Type 2, -- there is no footnote (k) to allow carriage in double hulled type 3 ships.<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Ethanol and Butanol appear in Ch 18 of the IBC code with MARPOL pollution category Z, meaning that they do not require to be carried in chemical tankers, but tanks used to carry the product must be capable to be stripped to the appriopriate level.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Biodiesel is a light to dark yellow liquid. It is inmixible in water and has high BP and low VP.&nbsp;&nbsp;It has a FP of around 150 deg C, making it rather inflammable. It has a SG of around 0.8.<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><br />\n</b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">FAME is readily cleaned from ships tanks. Some detergent must be used, as it is insoluble in water. They have lower viscosity than the corresponding oils they are derived from. They are liquid at ambient temperature. It can be regarded as a clean product. It&nbsp;&nbsp;presents no problems with regard to softening or absorption into tank coatings or with odour.<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><br />\n</b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">FAME derived from Palm/ Tallow/ Laurics must be carried at 25to 30 deg C range and discharged at 30 degC to 40 deg C range.<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><br />\n</b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Bio-alcohol is also called Butanol. It is alcohol obtained from biological sources like sugar or corn. It is mixed with gasoline in USA and called Gasohol.<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Band 1:&nbsp;&nbsp;75% or more petroleum oil and balance Biofuel</span></span><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 27.0pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">\u201cRenewable diesel\u201d is entered as&nbsp;&nbsp;\u201cAlkanes (C10</span></span><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">\u2010</span></span><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">C26) linear and branched\u201d as Cat Y&nbsp;&nbsp;in Type 3 ships.<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;
