sans-serif;\">Reacts with human tissue.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Neutralise acids<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Organic bases are flammable<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">A base which is soluble in water is called an alkali<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdgRmomh6I/AAAAAAAACaU/lmajd0Ts4sU/s1600/ph.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdgRmomh6I/AAAAAAAACaU/lmajd0Ts4sU/s1600/ph.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSiadydlUnI/AAAAAAAACmE/KAZf6Lp0ik4/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSiadydlUnI/AAAAAAAACmE/KAZf6Lp0ik4/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b><u><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Hydrocarbons</span></u></b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">:<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdRfdQzzwI/AAAAAAAACaQ/zL88fEmQf90/s1600/hc.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdRfdQzzwI/AAAAAAAACaQ/zL88fEmQf90/s1600/hc.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Hydrocarbons are divided into--<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">1) Aliphatic <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Chain like skeleton of C atoms, not arranged in ring structure, but open chains ( ethane )<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdNfx-9gdI/AAAAAAAACZg/pS0uc0_kJCk/s1600/aliphatic.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdNfx-9gdI/AAAAAAAACZg/pS0uc0_kJCk/s1600/aliphatic.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdNyBn_R9I/AAAAAAAACZk/rJip1Vevm4M/s1600/ethane.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdNyBn_R9I/AAAAAAAACZk/rJip1Vevm4M/s1600/ethane.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">2) Aromatic <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">( Rings of carbon atoms , Benzene, Toluene, Xylene ), sweetsmelling, Flammable, burn with smoky flames, stable, toxic, anaesthetic.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdOXm9C9OI/AAAAAAAACZo/uGXbeL96bvg/s1600/aromatic.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdOXm9C9OI/AAAAAAAACZo/uGXbeL96bvg/s1600/aromatic.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Aliphatic HC are further divide into\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">1) Alkanes<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Molecular formula: Cn H2n+2&nbsp;&nbsp; saturated HC containing single bond.&nbsp; No action on Potassium Permanganate. Also called Paraffin.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Ex: all ending in ane&nbsp; --Pentane, Butane, Hexane<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Ch4/ Methane<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">C2h6/ Ethane<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">C3h8/ Propane<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">C4h10/ Butane<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">C5h12/ Pentane<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">C6h14/ Hexane<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRR6L1yjsMI/AAAAAAAACTU/WRFCYaqnREI/s1600/images+%252844%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRR6L1yjsMI/AAAAAAAACTU/WRFCYaqnREI/s1600/images+%252844%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Thus when n=8, ( 2n+2)=18 and the Alkane is C8 H18 , it is called octane. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">It is one of the Alkanes in petrol.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdOt0dOmKI/AAAAAAAACZs/ARjV7kdRxZE/s1600/alkane.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdOt0dOmKI/AAAAAAAACZs/ARjV7kdRxZE/s1600/alkane.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Petroleum fractions and molecular composition of Alkanes present:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Gas/ C1 to C4<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">C5 to C7/ Petrol Ether<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">C5 to C9/ Motor Spirit<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">C9 to C10/ Naphtha<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">C10 to C16/ Kerosene<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">C10 to C18/ DO<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">C17 to C30/ HO<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">C15 to C50/ LO<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRR66eEkg0I/AAAAAAAACTY/X87N0l2WJEM/s1600/images+%252845%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRR66eEkg0I/AAAAAAAACTY/X87N0l2WJEM/s1600/images+%252845%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">2) Alkenes<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Mol formula Cn H2n&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; unsaturated HC containing double bond.&nbsp; Decolourises Potassium Permanganate<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Ex: all ending in ene<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Ethylene, Propelene, Pentene, Hexene <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdO-oE9y9I/AAAAAAAACZw/Wu8IhbAkYPU/s1600/cnh2n.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdO-oE9y9I/AAAAAAAACZw/Wu8IhbAkYPU/s1600/cnh2n.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdPIliWvoI/AAAAAAAACZ0/WF9CA5XEjlY/s1600/ane+ene+yne.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"90\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdPIliWvoI/AAAAAAAACZ0/WF9CA5XEjlY/s320/ane+ene+yne.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">3) Alkynes<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">MF: Cn H2n\u20132&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; unsaturated HC containing tripe bond<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"></div><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdPONZpv7I/AAAAAAAACZ4/HHSSs5vwCfM/s1600/alkyne+3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdPONZpv7I/AAAAAAAACZ4/HHSSs5vwCfM/s1600/alkyne+3.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"></div><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdPUepJn8I/AAAAAAAACZ8/cVdw5W_fsVo/s1600/alkyne.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"130\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdPUepJn8I/AAAAAAAACZ8/cVdw5W_fsVo/s320/alkyne.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">4) Cyclic Aliphatic<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">All starting with Cyclo and ending with ane/ ene<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdPoXi7OFI/AAAAAAAACaA/L5O8GA1n68k/s1600/cyclic.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdPoXi7OFI/AAAAAAAACaA/L5O8GA1n68k/s1600/cyclic.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Number of carbon atoms in HC:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">1/ Meth<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">2/ Eth<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">3/ Prop<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">4/ But<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">5/ Pent<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">6/Hex<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">7/Hept<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">8/Oct<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Proforma:&nbsp; SG/ BP/ MP<o:p></o:p></span></u></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Methane/ 0.42/ -160C/ -186C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Ethane/ 0.45/ -93C/ -172C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Propane/ 0.54/ -40C/ -814C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Butane/ 0.60/ 1C/ 135C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Pentane/ 0.63/ 36C/ -130C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">The smaller saturated HC methane, ethane , propane and butane are all colourless and odourless liquefied gases.&nbsp; They are all flammable and will burn in air to form CO2 and water.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-GxOuPLpzE2U/Tm7hPWiKwDI/AAAAAAAAGGU/eClbhbEdccQ/s1600/imagesCAEIJQH0.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-GxOuPLpzE2U/Tm7hPWiKwDI/AAAAAAAAGGU/eClbhbEdccQ/s1600/imagesCAEIJQH0.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-C3hAdeeKXi0/Tm7hTnO-axI/AAAAAAAAGGY/juFGPRmOANY/s1600/imagesCAWZO2DV.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"230\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-C3hAdeeKXi0/Tm7hTnO-axI/AAAAAAAAGGY/juFGPRmOANY/s320/imagesCAWZO2DV.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">HC contain only carbon and hydrogen atoms.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">4 carbon atoms in molecule/ gases at ambient temp / pressure ( propane )<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">5 to 20 carbon atoms/ liquid at ambient conditions&nbsp; ( octane )<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">&gt;20 carbon atoms/ solid at ambient conditions&nbsp; ( nonadecane )<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">A carbon atom has 4 bonds\u2014while a hydrogen atom has only one.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">For saturated HC the proportion of carbon and hydrogen atoms in the molecule will be in accordance with the gen formula of Cn H2n+2<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdP_hU6FRI/AAAAAAAACaE/MR8-1IxGsN0/s1600/cnh2n%252B2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdP_hU6FRI/AAAAAAAACaE/MR8-1IxGsN0/s1600/cnh2n%252B2.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdQzazsulI/AAAAAAAACaM/7BcaG8Yfg54/s1600/sat2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdQzazsulI/AAAAAAAACaM/7BcaG8Yfg54/s1600/sat2.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Thus methane CH4&nbsp; ethane C2H6 and propane C3H8 are all saturated HC<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-MKRQEPH719I/Tm7isjGrUGI/AAAAAAAAGGk/eFZFT9xAGYM/s1600/imagesCA2OK5W2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-MKRQEPH719I/Tm7isjGrUGI/AAAAAAAAGGk/eFZFT9xAGYM/s1600/imagesCA2OK5W2.jpg\" /></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdQmX9mOtI/AAAAAAAACaI/Ho8pv9c4yGI/s1600/sat.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdQmX9mOtI/AAAAAAAACaI/Ho8pv9c4yGI/s1600/sat.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Propylene C3H6 and butadiene C4H6 and ethylene C2H2 are unsaturated HC</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;
